  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1413b96c-686b-4d15-9527-def8613e80f1'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

<span id="freeTextContainer5178101195387385406">Fans of The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices can get to know warlock Magnus Bane like never before in this collection of New York Times bestselling tales, in print for the first time with an exclusive new story and illustrated material.<br/><br/>This collection of eleven short stories illuminates the life of the enigmatic Magnus Bane, whose alluring personality, flamboyan</span>
  <span id="freeText5178101195387385406" style="display:none">Fans of The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices can get to know warlock Magnus Bane like never before in this collection of New York Times bestselling tales, in print for the first time with an exclusive new story and illustrated material.<br /><br />This collection of eleven short stories illuminates the life of the enigmatic Magnus Bane, whose alluring personality, flamboyant style, and sharp wit populate the pages of the #1 New York Times bestselling series, The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices.<br /><br />Originally released one-by-one as e-only short stories by Cassandra Clare, Maureen Johnson, and Sarah Rees Brennan, this compilation presents all ten together in print for the first time and includes a never-before-seen eleventh tale, as well as new illustrated material.</span>

But the vampires don't mind... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17334066.What_to_Buy_the_Shadowhunter_Who_Has_Everything__The_Bane_Chronicles___8_" title="What to Buy the Shadowhunter Who Has Everything (The Bane Chronicles, #8) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">What to Buy the Shadowhunter Who Has Everything:</a>, Blurb: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Magnus Bane may or may not be dating Alec Lightwood, but he definitely needs to find him the perfect birthday present.<br><br>Set in the time between City of Ashes and City of Glass, warlock Magnus Bane is determined to find the best birthday present possible for Alec Lightwood, the Shadowhunter he may or may not be dating. And he’s also got to deal with the demon he’s conjured up for a very irritating client . . . <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17334061.The_Last_Stand_of_the_New_York_Institute__The_Bane_Chronicles___9_" title="The Last Stand of the New York Institute (The Bane Chronicles, #9) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Last Stand of the New York Institute</a>, Blurb: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Magnus meets Valentine in battle as the Circle attacks the Downworlders of New York City. <br><br>In the time of the Uprising, Valentine’s Circle goes after Downworlders in New York...and the Shadowhunters of the Institute must decide whether to join him, or fight with Magnus and his kind. This is the first time Magnus sees Jocelyn, Luke, and Stephen—but not the last. It is not long before Jocelyn seeks him out... <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17334065.The_Course_of_True_Love_and_First_Dates__The_Bane_Chronicles___10_" title="The Course of True Love and First Dates (The Bane Chronicles, #10) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Course of True Love and First Dates </a>, Blurb: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br><br>Magnus Bane and Alec Lightwood might fall in love—but first they have a first date. <br><br>When Magnus Bane, warlock, meets Alec Lightwood, Shadowhunter, sparks fly. And what happens on their first date lights a flame...  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><b>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer9474726967074993978">I so enjoyed my time reading <i>The Bane Chronicles</i>! This is one of the only books from <i>The Shadowhunter Chronicles</i> that I had not previously read more than once, so it was interesting to re-read it 4 years later!<br/><br/>I treasured getting to know Magnus better through his lifetime so much. It's fascinating how there is a distinct change in his character when comparing the stories where he is much younger and more care-free to tales of him being older, wiser, and more mature. I think the complexity of Mag</span>
  <span id="freeText9474726967074993978" style="display:none">I so enjoyed my time reading <i>The Bane Chronicles</i>! This is one of the only books from <i>The Shadowhunter Chronicles</i> that I had not previously read more than once, so it was interesting to re-read it 4 years later!<br /><br />I treasured getting to know Magnus better through his lifetime so much. It's fascinating how there is a distinct change in his character when comparing the stories where he is much younger and more care-free to tales of him being older, wiser, and more mature. I think the complexity of Magnus Bane is perfectly captured in this group of novellas and would absolutely recommend to anyone interested in gaining a larger history on his character.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer720296808195745084"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1538853995i/26411110._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Bones</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Ashes</a> ★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a> ★★★<br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br/>4.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br/>5.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br/>6.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br/><br/>I clutched my pearls so very tightly when I found out that there was an anthology that starred Magnus, my favorite character in all of Cassie Clare’s works. Magnus is the bisexual, Asian, warlock of my dreams, and I love him with every bone in my body. I truly believe he is on</span>
  <span id="freeText720296808195745084" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1538853995i/26411110._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br>5.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br>6.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br><br>I clutched my pearls so very tightly when I found out that there was an anthology that starred Magnus, my favorite character in all of Cassie Clare’s works. Magnus is the bisexual, Asian, warlock of my dreams, and I love him with every bone in my body. I truly believe he is one of the best characters in all of literature. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1539716801i/26459056._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Art from the tenth anniversary edition of <i>City of Bones</i>!) <br><br>I was a little apprehensive going in to this, because I didn’t realize that all of the stories were cowritten with other authors. But honestly? They blended together very well and read just like all the other Shadowhunter novels thus far. Each of these stories are about fifty pages long, but it was so much fun to dip my toes into all these different cities, years, and adventures. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2559269908" rel="nofollow noopener">The Midnight Heir</a> was easily, hands down, without question, my favorite story in this entire collection. And I am willing to grovel, beg, plead, maybe even commit a minor felony, to be able to learn more about James and Grace. (Oh my gosh, my lovely friend <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/62655595-lance" rel="nofollow noopener">Lance</a> just told me about <i>The Last Hours</i> and I’m happier than I’ve ever been!) But I am going to break down each short story with my thoughts, opinions, and individual star rating!<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2558101715" rel="nofollow noopener">What Really Happened in Peru</a>
</b> - ★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Humans did not live forever. They could only hope what they made would endure.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This follows Magnus and many of the different years that he spent in Peru. In 1791, with Ragnor Fell, and taverns, and monkeys, and pirates! Then we get to see Magnus in 1885 with Ragnor and Catarina, where Magnus is accepting a mysterious job. Then we jump to 1890 when Magnus meets Imasu and we get to see him drinking, riding magic carpets, mentioning people from TID, and falling in love. This was my favorite year, because there is just something so pure about seeing three very different warlocks coming together to talk about their lives, their demon fathers, and the expectations that have been placed upon them just by living a life that they didn’t ask for. Lastly, we see the year 1962, where Magnus meets a person named Kitty who is also a con-artist, a thief, and someone who is looking for love and adventure. And even though these little glimpses were fun, I was still just let down that we don’t truly know why Magnus was banned from Peru.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2558535909" rel="nofollow noopener">The Runaway Queen</a>
</b> - ★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“A count! Named Axel! A military man! With black hair and blue eyes! And in a state of distress! Oh, the universe had outdone herself.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This short story follows Magnus in Paris during the French Revolution in 1791. And apparently Paris is the place to be if you’re a vampire (which I highkey love, actually). Magnus attends a party with Henri de Polignac, then meets Axel von Fersen and accepts a difficult mission to smuggle Marie Antoinette and her family out of the city, before the desperate people take matters into their own hands. Of course, nothing goes as planned, and Magnus somehow acquires a pet monkey that he names Ragnor, but it was still a really enjoyable story and adventure. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2559157700" rel="nofollow noopener">Vampires, Scones, and Edmund Herondale</a>
</b> - ★★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I was born to be a warrior, and I was born to be with her.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Holy shit, all the stars! ALL THE STARS! I loved this one so much! Not only did we get to see Will’s parents, Edmund and Linette (which broke and warmed my heart), we got to see Woolsey’s older brother, Ralf, a baby Charlotte, Benedict Lightwood (yikes), some Morgensterns, and Camille herself (who I have honestly always liked)! This story surrounds a meeting were the downworlders are trying to make a treaty with the shadowhunters; but like always, the shadowhunters are shitty to them. But seeing so many faces, and so many relatives, of people that we know and love from TID – ahhh, I just loved it so much! This was perfection, and give me all the 1857, London Institute, stories with Magnus going on adventures with these people and fighting demons. Also, this story beautifully emphasizes the power of unconditional love and how it is always worth everything. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2559269908" rel="nofollow noopener">The Midnight Heir</a>
</b> - ★★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“…For one Herondale to be saved by love, and another Herondale dammed by it.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh my gosh, I loved this one so much, too! I mean, the Tessa, Will, and Jem cameos were perfection all on their own, but seeing their descendants? It still makes me feel equal parts heartbreak and love. Also, ever since finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a>, I have been obsessed with wanting to know more about the Blackthorns! In this story, Tatiana Blackthorn has called upon Magnus to do a terrible job, but before he finds his way to her abandoned garden estate, he finds a young James Herondale and has to escort him back to the London Institute. Friends, I’m not crying over this beautiful co-parenting triad; I’m weeping the happiest of tears. I loved this story so much, and my only complaint is that I hope we get more James and Grace in the future. Also, why does every Herondale just break my heart over and over again? I honestly do not understand.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2560485950" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rise of the Hotel Dumort</a>
</b> - ★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Nothing is permanent," Magnus said. "I know this from experience. But you can get new things. You can meet new people. You can go on.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I loved how this short story was set in 1929 New York, while Magnus is trying to run a speakeasy. And seeing his magic camouflage this secret pub into a tea party was pretty much the best thing ever. Sadly, that’s all I truly enjoyed about it. I mean, I guess seeing Hotel Dumort almost become a portal to Hell was pretty cool, too. But this story, and the new characters, just didn’t win me over as hard in this one.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2560486053" rel="nofollow noopener">Saving Raphael Santiago</a>
</b> - ★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Love did not overcome everything. Love did not always endure. All you had could be taken away, love could be the last thing you had, and then love could be taken too.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>My heart, my poor broken heart. This literally felt like torture to read after finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a>. Raphael Santiago was also a character that didn’t hide his pain and anger; and I always respected that. But everything he had to go through? Man, oh man. I will say that this story got pretty dark and <b>trigger warnings</b> for kidnapping, murder, and maybe even pedophilia. Louis is for sure the most evil person I’ve seen in the Shadowhunter world yet. Basically, in 1953, Magnus is a private detective, and Guadalupe, Raphael’s mother, hires him to find her son. This story just made me feel every single emotion. I also enjoyed seeing Hotel Dumort start to become the vampire lair. But the shining star of this book was obviously Raphael and his mother and the unconditional love that a mother should always have for her child. Ah, I didn’t ask for these tears all over again.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2562584982" rel="nofollow noopener">The Fall of the Hotel Dumort</a>
</b> - ★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Because in the end nothing is worse than seeing the fall of one you loved. It was somehow worse than losing a love. It made everything seem questionable. It made the past bitter and confused.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This was easily my least favorite in the collection. Like, it read like I was back in elementary school watching police officers tell us about the D.A.R.E campaign. Basically, this one is set is 1977 New York, and Camille and her vampires are getting high from drinking the blood of humans on drugs, and they get really addicted. I did enjoy the ending with the memory spell, but that was about it.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2562585596" rel="nofollow noopener">What to Buy the Shadowhunter Who Has Everything (And Who You're Not Officially Dating Anyway)</a>
</b> - ★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“This was love, new and bright and terrifying…”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Firstly, I will say that it’s really skeezy that Alec was indeed seventeen when he and Magnus started at least kissing one another. I don’t want to make light of that whatsoever, and I completely think it was wrong. But if you ignore that, I really loved this short story and seeing a glimpse in the Shadowhunter world before everything went down in TMI. I also really loved the scene with Izzy and Magnus; it was pure, perfect, and everything I’ve ever wanted. Also, I love how this heartfelt story was going on with a blue demon just hanging out in the apartment.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2562585999" rel="nofollow noopener">The Last Stand of the New York Institute</a>
</b> - ★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“It was one of the few things he had to believe in, the possibility of beauty when faced with the reality of so much ugliness.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The start of this novel and the homophobia really surprised me. I actually loved how Cassie Clare blatantly brought it up, rather than using metaphors with the oppression of the Downworlders, even though it hurt to see. But this short story also made me fall even more in love with Catarina, who is working at an HIV clinic because even people in the medical field can hold hateful prejudices. But the middle of this story, we got to see the behind the scenes start of Valentine and his (mostly) brainwashed circle. But the end of this story was the shining light! Seeing Tessa accept Clary with literal open arms made me tear up. Seeing her talk about her loves, her losses, and giving Jocelyn’s child a new start was really beautiful and made me very emotional. I loved this one, friends. <br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2563648929" rel="nofollow noopener">The Course of True Love (And First Dates) </a>
</b> - ★★★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“And silver, though few people knew it, was a rarer metal than gold.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh lord, this was adorable. This story shows Magnus and Alec’s first date and it was pretty sweet. Again, I will say that it is incredibly not okay that a 300+ year old warlock is dating a seventeen-year-old, but if you take that away from the equation then it was a really sweet and realistic depiction of an awkward and messy first date. Well, besides going to bar and having to fight a werewolf together.<br><br>➽ <b>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2563649352" rel="nofollow noopener">The Voicemail of Magnus Bane</a>
</b> - ★★<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Please don’t ever tell Jace I said he was a badass.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This short story is just a transcript of voicemails that the Shadowhunters left for Magnus after the end of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Lost Souls</a>, when he and Alec broke up. It just wasn’t enjoyable and was a lot of harassment even though I know that it was coming from a place of good. I just, thought this was honestly a bit pointless, but I know it was supposed to be heartwarming. I will also say that I think it was a really poor choice for a concluding story, because it for sure finished the entire anthology on a low note.<br><br>I gave <i>The Bane Chronicles</i> three stars overall, because out of a possible 55 stars (5 stars possible for each of the 11 stories) this collection accumulated 35 stars <b>(~63%)</b>! But I really do think this is such an important addition to this world, and I very much feel like it is a necessary read. Even if it just means that you get to meet James Herondale. <br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> <br><br>Buddy read with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7285286-nana" rel="nofollow noopener">Lea</a> at <a href="https://www.youtube.com/user/drumsofautumn" rel="nofollow noopener">drumsofautumn</a>! ❤</span>
  <a data-text-id="720296808195745084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer10132755483057367525">This book, unfortunately, did nothing for me.<br/><br/>I remember Magnus Bane being one of my favorite characters of the original TMI series (if you can remember that far back, with all of Clare's publications and planned publications since then), but it's been so long since I read <i>City of Lost Souls</i> that all of my emotional attachment to him has disintegrated into ash.<br/><br/>For someone more connected to this series than I am, this may be a great addition, full of intriguing backstory and unique Magnus humor. B</span>
  <span id="freeText10132755483057367525" style="display:none">This book, unfortunately, did nothing for me.<br /><br />I remember Magnus Bane being one of my favorite characters of the original TMI series (if you can remember that far back, with all of Clare's publications and planned publications since then), but it's been so long since I read <i>City of Lost Souls</i> that all of my emotional attachment to him has disintegrated into ash.<br /><br />For someone more connected to this series than I am, this may be a great addition, full of intriguing backstory and unique Magnus humor. But for me, this book was minimally funny and minimally entertaining. 2 gracious stars.<br /><br /><br /><br /><br />_______________________________________________<br /><br /><br /><b>Original Pre-Review:</b><br /><br />This woman will never stop.<br /><br />Ever.<br /><br />Next thing you know, there's going to be an e-book series about the damn cat. And there's going to be a trilogy about when Simon was a rat.<br /><br />I am done.</span>

<div id="review_572860304" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572860304" />
    <a title="Matilda" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16071454-matilda"><img alt="Matilda" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1372798243p2/16071454.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572860304?book_show_action=true">Mar 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Matilda" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Matilda" href="/user/show/16071454-matilda">Matilda</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572860304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17004826051585442630">I feel like I enjoyed this more by reading them all together. <br/><br/><br/>Woah looking through the comments all I can see is hate....for Cassandra Clare and how she is milking the fanchise,for a start:<br/>STOP if you dont want to read another one her books you don't have to- we are not making you! People who actually want to read her book can buy them and read them and LOVE THEM. <br/>I love the Shadow Hunter world and I dont think there is any problem with so many books being out. I love the world and charaters and</span>
  <span id="freeText17004826051585442630" style="display:none">I feel like I enjoyed this more by reading them all together. <br /><br /><br />Woah looking through the comments all I can see is hate....for Cassandra Clare and how she is milking the fanchise,for a start:<br />STOP if you dont want to read another one her books you don't have to- we are not making you! People who actually want to read her book can buy them and read them and LOVE THEM. <br />I love the Shadow Hunter world and I dont think there is any problem with so many books being out. I love the world and charaters and there is no end to what I want to read about them. If I do one day not want to read about it anymore I will stop, I won't shout and tell everyone how she is milking the series. I just wouldn't read them at all.<br />Stop hating it- no ones forcing you.<br /><br />Sorry for that rant just all the haters rant about it saying how she's milking it when most, if not all, of them will buy this book! <br />I AM SUPER LOOKING FORWARD TO THIS BOOK!<br /><br />Now I know everyone will be like "Your allowed your own opinion" and I agree with that but the amount of hate is like WOAH!!!</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer7325900278877310601"><i>"There was also the fact that sometimes vampires commited crimes worse than murder. They committed crimes against fashion."</i><br/><br/>A few years ago I was super excited about this being released. I couldn't wait to get more of Magnus.<br/>Today I'm bored and annoyed. Magnus is such a sissy. So shallow. Such a typical Clare character. I honestly can't stand her pretentious plots/characters anymore. I can't keep from rolling my eyes and groaning(see quote above). Which is one of the reasons why it took me half a</span>
  <span id="freeText7325900278877310601" style="display:none"><i>"There was also the fact that sometimes vampires commited crimes worse than murder. They committed crimes against fashion."</i><br /><br />A few years ago I was super excited about this being released. I couldn't wait to get more of Magnus.<br />Today I'm bored and annoyed. Magnus is such a sissy. So shallow. Such a typical Clare character. I honestly can't stand her pretentious plots/characters anymore. I can't keep from rolling my eyes and groaning(see quote above). Which is one of the reasons why it took me half a year to finish this book.<br /><br />I really enjoy short stories that let you see more of your favourite books. A little prequel there, a scene told from another POV. But you can also kill a story with too much information. I need room for imagination. And Clare fills every freaking space with hers. It's real, she loves her own characters so much, she's her own biggest fan and she needs to calm down.<br /><br />Now, this doesn't mean it was all bad. Because there's Alec and then there's Isabelle and they're my favourite characters in this series. The cute little scenes between Magnus and Alec made me giggle and smile. I'm so glad for their existence.<br /><br />Honestly, Cassandra Clare needs to cut the crap and get it over with. I just can't deal with self-absorbed, self-loathing, tragic, secretly good-hearted and loving characters with unnaturally beautiful faces and the same boring sass anymore. Because that pretty much sums it all up. Every single one of them.<br /><br />I doubt it comes as a surprise that I will not be reading the Bane trilogy.<br /><br /><a href="https://www.instagram.com/fantasticbooksandwheretofindem/" rel="nofollow noopener">Find more of my books on Instagram</a></span>

<div id="review_476072727" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476072727" />
    <a title="Rayne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5374178-rayne"><img alt="Rayne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1440598663p2/5374178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476072727?book_show_action=true">Dec 12, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rayne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rayne" href="/user/show/5374178-rayne">Rayne</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer476072727" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6161519730118274625">So, back in the end of 2007, I was one of 'those' girls. You know, the ones that built shrines for Clare's writing ability, who desperately wanted to live in the world she created and the ones that proclaimed City of Bones as the best book evah?! <---Yeah. That annoying chick. Trust me, I regret it.<br/><br/>I want to use the "I was young and stupid" excuse and the "I didn't know good quality YA back then", and although they are valid and certainly true, the thing is, I do like The Mortal Instruments (min</span>
  <span id="freeText6161519730118274625" style="display:none">So, back in the end of 2007, I was one of 'those' girls. You know, the ones that built shrines for Clare's writing ability, who desperately wanted to live in the world she created and the ones that proclaimed City of Bones as the best book evah?! &lt;---Yeah. That annoying chick. Trust me, I regret it.<br /><br />I want to use the "I was young and stupid" excuse and the "I didn't know good quality YA back then", and although they are valid and certainly true, the thing is, I do like The Mortal Instruments (minus the last two installments, but I'll get to that). At first I wasn't that interested in the book, but City of Bones grabbed my attention and earned my genuine affection, and although I really, really want to lower the rating or take it out of my favorites because now I acknowledge how flawed the books are, I won't because I would be betraying a part of myself that will always have an appreciation for these books. <br /><br />Having said that, I really, really want Clare to just freaking stop. As someone who is somewhat of a fan of all of her books, one would think I am eagerly expecting more and more installments in this franchise. But the truth is that I am sick and tired of this. I keep spending my money on expensive hardcovers just so that I can feel like I've been slapped in the face with the mediocrity of the storyline and storytelling, as was the case with the expansion of The Mortal Instrument: City of Fallen Angels and City of Lost Souls, or to feel betrayed by the glaring similarities between The Mortal Instruments and The Infernal Devices. And now another trilogy is coming? A new compilation of essays? A guide on the world of the Shadowhunters? Another compilation of short stories? No. Please, just no. <br /><br />It's almost like Clare is a one-trick pony. Move on! Prove you can do something else! I know it's hard to invest so much time in the creation of such a complex world, but you need to let go and improve yourself as a writer. J.K. Rowling built one of the best and most complex worlds in the history of literature. She told her story and she was done, because she knew that, as a writer, she can do more and it is also her responsibility to do more.<br /><br />The more I think about this, the angrier I get and the less I like her books, so I'll just leave it a that. I might check this out, but I won't promise anything. After I'm done with Clockwork Princess, I don't plan on following any other Shadowhunter any time soon. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6161519730118274625" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_474834770" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/474834770" />
    <a title="Kameron B. Moore" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6268473-kameron-b-moore"><img alt="Kameron B. Moore" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524080698p2/6268473.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/474834770?book_show_action=true">Dec 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kameron B. Moore" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kameron B. Moore" href="/user/show/6268473-kameron-b-moore">Kameron B. Moore</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6268473-kameron-b-moore?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6268473-kameron-b-moore?shelf=auto-buy">auto-buy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6268473-kameron-b-moore?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer474834770" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1933164508353541410">WHY IS EVERYONE HATING ON CASSANDRA CLARE BECAUSE SHE HAS A NEW BOOK COMING OUT? There is no reason everyone should be saying the stuff they are saying on here. Yes, everyone's entitled to their opinion, but I've read some reviews that say she bullied people in her past, well, the things those people have been saying can be considered as bullying. And who cares if she did it in her past?! Past is past. And it's her life; she doesn't have to tell the entire world about what she's done in the past</span>
  <span id="freeText1933164508353541410" style="display:none">WHY IS EVERYONE HATING ON CASSANDRA CLARE BECAUSE SHE HAS A NEW BOOK COMING OUT? There is no reason everyone should be saying the stuff they are saying on here. Yes, everyone's entitled to their opinion, but I've read some reviews that say she bullied people in her past, well, the things those people have been saying can be considered as bullying. And who cares if she did it in her past?! Past is past. And it's her life; she doesn't have to tell the entire world about what she's done in the past! I bet everyone who has been saying she is a bully and is stupid and has done really bad things in the past, have done something really stupid in THEIR past! Do you go around and tell EVERYONE about it? No. So why should Cassandra Clare have to do it? And so what if she is making A LOT of series about her world. IT IS HER WORLD. She can do with it what she wants. She can write 10 different series with the same concept. It is not our decision about what she writes. So far, she's only written three series (The Mortal Instruments, The Infernal Devices, The Bane Chronicles). She is planning to write three more series (The Dark Artifices, The Wicked Powers, TLH). SO WHAT? She can write what she pleases. And if no one has realized, she is writing a series with her friend, Holly Black, called The Magisterium (WHICH IS NOT A RIP OFF OF HARRY POTTER! IT ONLY HAS A SIMILAR IDEA! TOTALLY DIFFERENT EXECUTION!) Ok, I think I have made my point. Please just stop hating on Cassandra Clare, and think about what you write, before you post it on Goodreads or anywhere else. That is my opinion...</span>

  <span id="freeText9688411281139522605" style="display:none">1.) <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=D-C_nSVOQkg" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★★<br />2.) <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=uYah8OfkFeo&amp;t=" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★★★<br />3.) <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_1fFdgJHL6A" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★★<br />4.) Ghosts of the Shadow Market ★★★★<br /><br />-----------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>What Really Happened in Peru</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 3 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>”That was what humans did: They left one another messages through time, pressed between pages or carved into rock. Like reaching out a hand through time, and trusting in a phantom hoped-for hand to catch yours.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Kinda boring, kinda funny, kinda heartbreaking. <br /><br /><b>The Runaway Queen</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 3 . 5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“When one steals a flying balloon and animates it to fly over Paris, one should, ideally, have some idea how said balloon normally works.”</b>
</i><br /><br />This was interesting! Best part was the monkey lol. <br /><br /><br /><b>Vampires, Scones and Edmund Herondale</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“One can give up many things for love, but one should not give up oneself.”</b>
</i><br /><br />I totally forgot that we get a story on Will and Cecily’s parents meeting for the first time! Ow, my heart. <br /><br /><b>The Midnight Heir</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“How they loved each other, these three, how they had suffered for each other, and yet how much joy they clearly took from simply being in the same room.”</b>
</i><br /><br />My, oh, my. Mr James Herondale, why you gotta be such an asshat? Also Grace is creepy as hell. I can’t wait to read more about these characters in Chain of Gold!<br /><br /><br /><b>The Rise of the Hotel Dumort</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 2.5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Nothing is permanent," Magnus said. "I know this from experience. But you can get new things. You can meet new people. You can go on.”</b>
</i><br /><br />This one was SO BORING up until the last few pages. <br /><br /><b>Saving Raphael Santiago</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4.5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“He had such a sweet face, Magnus thought -the face of an innocent angel, and the soul of the crankiest person in the entire world.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Raphael is one of my absolute favourite characters, so of course I loved this story &lt;3<br /><br /><b>The Fall of the Hotel Dumort</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 2.5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“When you love someone that intensely and they do not love you in the same way, it is impossible to part well.”</b>
</i><br /><br />yeahhhhh I don’t really have anything to say about this one? <br /><br /><b>What To Buy The Shadowhunter Who Has Everything</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4.5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“This was love, new and bright and terrifying.”</b>
</i><br /><br />I loved this one so much!! Elyaas the demon is my fave. Raphael and Lily are my faves. Magnus and Alec are my faves. My heart is full! <br /><br /><b>The Last Stand of the New York Institute</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>”He had seen many monsters who could love, but only a few who had let that love change them, who had been able to alchemize love for one person into kindness for many.”</b>
</i><br /><br />Owwwwww my heart. Also, I still hate Robert Lightwood with a passion. <br /><br /><b>The Course of True Love (And First Dates)</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4.5 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“Magnus had heard the story of how the Nephilim were created many times. They must have forgotten to leave out the bit that said: And the Angel descended from on high and gave his chosen ones fantastic abs.”</b>
</i><br /><br />I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them I love them.<br /><br /><b>The Voicemail of Magnus Bane</b><br />✧·ﾟ: ✧·ﾟ: 4 s t a r s :·ﾟ✧:·ﾟ✧<br /><br /><i>
  <b>“I have looked back on portraits of our ancestors. Gabriel Lightwood was notably smoking. It is rumored that one Consul agreed with everything my great-great aunt Felicia Lightwood ever said, because when she spoke all he heard was ‘Foxy foxy foxy.’ If you break up with Alec, you will not<br />only be losing one stone cold fox, but a family of foxes. I will pass down the word to my children’s children. No Lightwood is ever going to so much as wink at you in a bar. Think about that. Think about being Lightwoodless and lonely five hundred years from now, in a sad and chilly nightclub on the moon.”</b>
</i><br /><br />I was honestly expecting this one to be a waste of time, but it was hilarious! Isabelle Lightwood is a comedy queen! <br /><br />FINAL RATING: 3.7 stars</span>

<div id="review_572745598" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/572745598" />
    <a title=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/703854-rebecca"><img alt=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1529467844p2/703854.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572745598?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name=" ♥ Rebecca ♥" href="/user/show/703854-rebecca"> ♥ Rebecca ♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=magic">magic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=extras">extras</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=own-physical-copy">own-physical-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/703854-rebecca?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572745598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5346841462125338489">This review can also be found on my blog: <a href='http://amatchmadeinheavenreviews.blogspot.ca/2015/01/the-bane-chronicles-by-cassandra-clare.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>A Match Made in Heaven</a><br/><br/>So, some background on my relationship with Cassie. I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/256683.City_of_Bones__The_Mortal_Instruments___1_' title='City of Bones (The Mortal Instruments, #1) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Bones</a> first. Wasn't a huge fan of it, didn't particularly like Clary or Jace, I hated their relationship, and I hated Simon. The only redeeming quality was the excellent world-building and Magnus Bane. As I read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1582996.City_of_Ashes__The_Mortal_Instruments___2_' title='City of Ashes (The Mortal Instruments, #2) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Ashes</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3777732.City_of_Glass__The_Mortal_Instruments___3_' title='City of Glass (The Mortal Instruments, #3) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a> I felt the same way and decided that was a good place to stop. I have never read <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6752378.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_' title='City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a>.<br/><br/>Then, as I heard all t</span>
  <span id="freeText5346841462125338489" style="display:none">This review can also be found on my blog: <a href="http://amatchmadeinheavenreviews.blogspot.ca/2015/01/the-bane-chronicles-by-cassandra-clare.html" rel="nofollow noopener">A Match Made in Heaven</a><br><br>So, some background on my relationship with Cassie. I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/256683.City_of_Bones__The_Mortal_Instruments___1_" title="City of Bones (The Mortal Instruments, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> first. Wasn't a huge fan of it, didn't particularly like Clary or Jace, I hated their relationship, and I hated Simon. The only redeeming quality was the excellent world-building and Magnus Bane. As I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1582996.City_of_Ashes__The_Mortal_Instruments___2_" title="City of Ashes (The Mortal Instruments, #2) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/3777732.City_of_Glass__The_Mortal_Instruments___3_" title="City of Glass (The Mortal Instruments, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> I felt the same way and decided that was a good place to stop. I have never read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6752378.City_of_Fallen_Angels__The_Mortal_Instruments___4_" title="City of Fallen Angels (The Mortal Instruments, #4) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a>.<br><br>Then, as I heard all the ravings from fans about how much better TID was, and all the raving about Will and Jem, I became curious and wanted to know which side of the love-triangle I would fall on. So I read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7171637.Clockwork_Angel__The_Infernal_Devices___1_" title="Clockwork Angel (The Infernal Devices, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> and yes, it is much better. It introduced me to Jem, who is one of the best things Cassie has ever created, the story was very interesting, and Tessa is somewhat better than Clary. At least I don't actively dislike her. But there is one major drawback. Will Herondale is one of the worst things I have ever seen created on paper. I cant even tell you have much I hate him because words do not suffice.<br><br>I am always somewhat scared to start a new Cassie Clare book because her world is amazing and it has a lot of potential to impress me but I just seem to hate what she seems to think is a good romance and a good romantic lead. I do intend to keep trying though, by reading each of her new series. But as I said, Magnus Bane is one of the redeeming characters she has created, and I was excited to read about him in his own world.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526783633ra/25568623.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Each story in this book was interesting in its own right. I won't say which was my favourite because they were all interesting, entertaining, funny, and they all taught me something new about Magnus Bane. That is the best thing about this book. The overall experience of getting to know Magnus Bane better. He never received this kind of undivided attention before and I feel like I know him intimately now. I don't know how much he appeared in the latter books of TMI, but this gave me a whole new view of him and I love him even more. He is an amazing warlock and an amazing person. <br><br>I loved seeing the friends he made over the years, the lovers, how he treated people, including Shadowhunters; how he tried to save Raphael, Camille, and innocent werewolf families. He is a hero. But he never stops being Magnus either. He shows up to battle in hot pink. I love his sense of humour too, his sarcasm. That is something I already knew about him, but I really enjoyed seeing more of it. Two side of him worth loving. <br><br>I also loved seeing him with Alec. I enjoyed Alec in the books as well, but its different when you see him as Magnus sees him. I never knew Alec was so insecure and shy and good. I loved the way Magnus described him and the way he made him feel. It makes me reconsider finishing TMI, just to get a few more glimpses of Magnus and Alec together. I now have an incredible love and respect for Magnus Bane. I love him more than this series can contain. He is too big for his world. I will keep trying with Cassie Clare, but I have no reason to expect to find anything as great as this by her in the future.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5346841462125338489" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

(Yes, even after reading this book). As his stan, I felt like his portrayal in this book was extremely bad.<br/><b>I was looking forward</b> to my favourite, bisexual warlock with an amazing sense of humour and also maybe his "shiny, glittery" personality.<br/><b> What I got </b>was an insight into his one-dimensional and childish mind and I </span>
  <span id="freeText1694732735917983103" style="display:none"><b> <u>Book 1: </u></b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17334079.What_Really_Happened_in_Peru__The_Bane_Chronicles___1_" title="What Really Happened in Peru (The Bane Chronicles, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">What Really Happened in Peru</a><br /><br />Unsatisfactory Drivel. <br /><br />Be it <i> The Infernal Devices </i> or <i> The Mortal Instruments </i>, Magnus Bane was my favourite character and he will always be. (Yes, even after reading this book). As his stan, I felt like his portrayal in this book was extremely bad.<br /><b>I was looking forward</b> to my favourite, bisexual warlock with an amazing sense of humour and also maybe his "shiny, glittery" personality.<br /><b> What I got </b>was an insight into his one-dimensional and childish mind and I KNOW that's not who he is or that the author(s) didn't intend to portray him that way, but that's what it felt like. <br />Sure, it was funny but do all the chuckles produced overpower the slow and poorly written plot? I don't think so. <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText9413837370586671732" style="display:none">This is the oldest book on my TBR so I finally decided to pick it up on audiobook. And i'm so disappointed :( Had I read this back in 2013 when I got it, back when I was still OBSESSED with TMI, i'm sure I would have loved it. But now I've forgotten literally all of the characters and events and this provides no context and it's just random vignettes of Magnus's life. The entire reason I took off as many stars as I did is because I was booooored. I skim read a ton of stories and put the audiobook on 2.5 times speed as I scrolled Tumblr just to slog through it. I only enjoyed 3 stories out of this, but even those were only like 3 stars individually. I would advise skipping this unless you're reading the entire shadowhunters chronicles and read this right with TMI/TID.</span>

<div id="review_3084471049" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3084471049" />
    <a title="Lena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/68387169-lena"><img alt="Lena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1587934816p2/68387169.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3084471049?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lena" href="/user/show/68387169-lena">Lena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68387169-lena?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68387169-lena?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/68387169-lena?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3084471049" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer433164707725926938">Wow... that really was something. Not gonna lie the first half of this book is freaking terrible. I was tempted to quit it, a thing that had never happened to me while reading a Cassandra Clare book. <br/>Well, besides while reading <i> 'The Shadowhunter Codex' </i> of course, but I am just going to pretend that the Codex doesn't exist. Luckily, the second half of the book got way better. There were some really good short stories, but to get to the good parts was really a struggle. Like, seriously, who let </span>
  <span id="freeText433164707725926938" style="display:none">Wow... that really was something. Not gonna lie the first half of this book is freaking terrible. I was tempted to quit it, a thing that had never happened to me while reading a Cassandra Clare book. <br />Well, besides while reading <i> 'The Shadowhunter Codex' </i> of course, but I am just going to pretend that the Codex doesn't exist. Luckily, the second half of the book got way better. There were some really good short stories, but to get to the good parts was really a struggle. Like, seriously, who let Clare publish this half-baked mess? <br /><br /><b> What really happened in Peru: 1 star </b><br />Definitely the worst one of the bunch. All this little short stories in one chapter where just way to much, also it was boring as hell. <br /><br /><b> The Runaway Queen: 2 stars </b><br />Better than the first one but still kinda meh. Basically it's just Marie Antoinetts life story copied with Magnus Bane in it.<br /><br /><b> Vampires, Scones and Edmund Herondale: 3 stars </b><br />I'm kinda over hearing stories about a brave, tragic-hero Herondales, who acts exactly like Jace. Why not make someone else the hero? I would love to read a story where a Morgenstern or a Lovelace is the hero (also I am sure that there must have been a evil, grumpy Herondale or a huge jerk Herondale somewhere in the Shadowhunter history)<br /><br /><b> The Midnight Heir: 3 stars </b><br />Oh well, there we go again with another not-Jace-but-still-acts-like-him Herondal. I really liked Jamie's story in <i> 'Tales of the Shadowhunter Academy' </i> (mostly because of Matthew, who, sadly, was only mentioned in this one), but I am kinda over it. The story was good execpt for the sudden ending, which felt like something was missing.<br /><br /><b> The Rise of the Hotel Dumort: 3 stars </b><br />I usually love everything about the 1920s, but the story was still kinda basic.<br /><br /><b> Saving Raphael Santiago: 4 stars </b><br />Yessss, finally a good one! Raphael is such an underrated character.<br /><br /><b> Fall of the Hotel Dumort: 4 stars </b><br />It was OK. At this point I am so desperate for another good chapter that I am going with 4 stars, even if it is probably closer to 3 stars. <br /><br /><b> What To Buy The Shadowhunter Who Has Everything (And Who You're Not Officially Dating Anyway): 4 stars </b><br />Alec is such a cutie he really deserves the world. Fight me. <br /><br /><b> The Last Stand of the New York Institute: 4 stars </b><br />The killing of the Shadowhunter family was kinda unnecessary, but I loved to read about Magnus and Jocelyn's first meeting.<br /><br /><b> The Course of True Love (and First Dates): 5 stars </b><br />This might be my fav! Alec being a cutie part 2<br /><br /><b> The Voicemail of Magnus Bane: 5 stars as well </b> <br />Pretty short, but also pretty funny. It's an awesome way to end the book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="433164707725926938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer6333688368212913088"><blockquote>
<b><i>“Have a little faith in my magic fingers” </i></b> </blockquote><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456965939ra/18301764.gif' width='400' height='200' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>Magnus</i> is a character that I always liked. I enjoyed it in <i>TID trilogy</i>, while he helped Will and I loved it in <i>TMI series</i> with all his eccentricity and his love for <i>Alec</i> <s>although he seemed a little stalker sometimes</s>.It is a fascinating character, one of those who always brings light to a scene and even can make you laugh at the most tragic moments.<br/><br/><blockquote>
<b><i>“Magnus did not have enormous respect for the Law, but if he was breaking it he wanted to look good doing</i></b></blockquote></span>

<b><i>“Have a little faith in my magic fingers” </i></b> </blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1456965939ra/18301764.gif" width="400" height="200" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>Magnus</i> is a character that I always liked. I enjoyed it in <i>TID trilogy</i>, while he helped Will and I loved it in <i>TMI series</i> with all his eccentricity and his love for <i>Alec</i> <s>although he seemed a little stalker sometimes</s>.It is a fascinating character, one of those who always brings light to a scene and even can make you laugh at the most tragic moments.<br><br><blockquote>

<b><i>“To them, as to Magnus, time was like rain, glittering as it fell, changing the world, but something that could also be taken for granted.<br>Until you loved a mortal. Then time became gold in a miser's hands, every bright year counted out carefully, infinitely precious, and each one slipping through your fingers.” <br></i></b> </blockquote><br>This is something I've always liked, personally: He's constantly showing up the price of his immortality, he doesn't make it looks like something great, but as a constant journey where death and the loss of the loved ones is something to overcome continually .<br>Also, I enjoyed a lot of reading his encounters with some other beloved characters as <i>Will, Tessa and Raphael!</i><b>

It is a book highly recommended for anyone who has read any of those series!</i>
